				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Symphony in C-sharp minor, B.29 (Bloch, Ernest)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><table class="toccolours protected" style="border: 1px solid #8888aa; padding-top:4px; padding-bottom:4px; padding-left:8px; padding-right:8px; font-size:95%;">

<tr>
<td align="justify">
<p>This work is <b><i>likely not</i></b> in the <a href="/wiki/Public_Domain" title="Public Domain" class="mw-redirect">public domain</a> in the US (due to first publication with the required notice after 1922, plus renewal or "restoration" under the GATT/TRIPS amendments), nor in the EU and those countries where the copyright term is life+70 years. However, it <b><i>is</i> <a href="/wiki/Public_Domain" title="Public Domain" class="mw-redirect">public domain</a></b> in Canada (where IMSLP is hosted) and in other countries (China, Japan, S. Korea) where the copyright term is life+50 years.
</p>
<center><span style="color:crimson"><b>Please obey the copyright laws of your country. IMSLP does not assume any sort of legal responsibility or liability for the consequences of downloading files that are not in the public domain in your country.</b></span></center>
</td></tr></table>

<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>*E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span> clarinet part is the transposed part for today's D clarinet part (in the Clarinet 2 part). In this case, there is still only 3 clarinets + bass clarinet playing, not 4 clarinet parts playing.
</td></tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>Bloch ended up composing several symphonies (some with title - "America", "Israel" - some without - Symphony in E-flat major, Symphony for Trombone and Orchestra, Sinfonia Breve - at least 6&#160;?)
</p><p>It seems of all of them, this is the 2nd, as a first dating from around 1897 remains in manuscript. The last, after the E-flat symphony, was left incomplete (it seems?...)
</p>
